# They/Them Siri Shortcut Documentation ## A quick utility to demonstrate use of They/Them pronouns. [**GitHub Documentation**](https://github.com/extratone/i/issues/113) *** ## About This shortcut was created for the next time you encounter the sentence ‚Äúit just doesn‚Äôt sound right,‚Äù or variations, regarding they/them pronouns. It opens [prounouns.is‚Äô handy explainer](http://pronoun.is/they/.../themselves) in Safari, copies the URL to the clipboard, and then plays an audio clip of Siri Voice 3 reading aloud said webpage‚Äôs examples. I personally have the shortcut named ‚Äúthey‚Äù so I can use type-to-siri‚Äôs CLI-ish function *or* simply ‚ÄúHey Siri!‚Ä¶ They.‚Äù *** ## Contact * [Contact Card](https://bit.ly/whoisdavidblue) * [Telegram](https://t.me/extratone) * [Email](mailto:davidblue@extratone.com) * [Twitter](https://twitter.com/NeoYokel) * [Mastodon](https://mastodon.social/@DavidBlue) * [Discord](https://discord.gg/0b9KQUKP858b0iZF) * [*Everywhere*](https://raindrop.io/davidblue/social-directory-21059174)...
Rose Astra is the creator of pronouns.is. Thank you, Rose! (Now YOU say it, user. üò¨) https://twitter.com/morganastra
